country_event = {
	id = 71801
	title = "Dynamic Loc Province Bounce Event"
	picture = "crisis"
	allow_multiple_instances = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		UTI = { set_variable = { which = itterator value = 0 } }
		any_land_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = slot_1_province
			}
			UTI = { change_variable = { which = itterator value = 2 } }
		}
		any_land_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = slot_2_province
			}
			UTI = { change_variable = { which = itterator value = 3 } }

				has_province_modifier = slot_3_province

			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = slot_4_province

			UTI = { change_variable = { which = itterator value = 5 } }

			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = slot_5_province

		}
		any_land_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = slot_19_province
			}
			UTI = { change_variable = { which = itterator value = 20 } }
		}
		any_land_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = slot_20_province
			}
			UTI = { change_variable = { which = itterator value = 21 } }
		}
		country_event = 71802
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ""
	}
}
